[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA Jazzer fuzzing session against the Apache Tika RTF parser triggered a [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`FuzzerSecurityIssueHigh` exception indicating a potential remote code execution [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerability. The fuzzer input exercised Tika’s RTF embedded-object handler, which[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeserializes data from the RTF stream without apparent restrictions on class or [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mobject creation. As a result, untrusted RTF content could lead to instantiation of [0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue Manifestation  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  During the execution of `com.example.RTFParserFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`, Jazzer [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreported a high-severity security finding:  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  `com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueHigh: Remote Code Execution`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The stack trace shows that the finding is reported from [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mjaz.Zer.reportFinding[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` after untrusted data is passed into an [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ObjectInputStream`.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The finding corresponds to a remote code execution [0m[1;39m([0m[39mRCE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m risk arising from [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munchecked deserialization and unrestricted class/object creation. This matches [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcommon Java deserialization vulnerabilities.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key Observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The crash originates in [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`org.apache.tika.parser.microsoft.rtf.RTFEmbObjHandler.handleCompletedObject` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline[0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The deserialization path flows through `RTFEmbObjHandler` → [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`TextExtractor.processGroupEnd` → `TextExtractor.extract` → [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`RTFParser.parseInline`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`parse` → the fuzzing harness.  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`RTFParserFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m merely feeds input to Tika and is not itself [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerable; it simply drives the parser into the problematic code path.  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Jazzer flags the issue because the deserialized data originates from external [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mfuzzer-supplied[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m input, enabling creation of arbitrary classes depending on the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mruntime classpath.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code Areas for Investigation  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  To obtain a holistic view of the issue, the following components should be [0m       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1470[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtika-parsers/tika-parsers-standard/tika-parsers-standard-modules/tika-parser-micros[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moft-module/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/parser/microsoft/rtf/RTFEmbObjHandler.jav[0m[1;92ma[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m:97[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m105[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m97[0m[39m:    protected void [0m[1;35mstartObjData[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                              [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m100[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m101[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m102[0m[39m:    protected void [0m[1;35mstartJavaObjData[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m103[0m[39m:        state = EMB_STATE.JAVA_OBJDATA;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m104[0m[39m:        metadata = new [0m[1;35mMetadata[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m105[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtika-parsers/tika-parsers-standard/tika-parsers-standard-modules/tika-parser-micros[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moft-module/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/parser/microsoft/rtf/GroupState.jav[0m[1;92ma:36[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m39[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m36[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[95min[0m[39m objdata[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m37[0m[39m:    public boolean objdata;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m38[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[95min[0m[39m javaobjdata[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m39[0m[39m:    public boolean javaobjdata;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter reviewing the report and the RTF-embedded‐object handling code, the root [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcause is the unfiltered use of [0m[1;35mjava.io.ObjectInputStream.readObject[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m on [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattacker-controlled data [0m[1;39m([0m[39mEMB_STATE.JAVA_OBJDATA[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. To close this RCE vector while [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreserving RTF parsing functionality, we propose the following approach:[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Centralize Deserialization Entry Point[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Create a new helper class in the `org.apache.tika.parser.microsoft.rtf` [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpackage, e.g. `SecureObjectInputStream`, that extends ObjectInputStream [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfor Java [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m8[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and/or configures an `ObjectInputFilter` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfor Java [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m+[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Within `SecureObjectInputStream`, override `[0m[1;35mresolveClass[0m[1;39m([0m[39mObjectStreamClass [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdesc[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mJava [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m path[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to enforce a strict whitelist of allowed classes [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g. only [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprimitive wrappers and String[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - For Java [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m+, call `[0m[1;35msetObjectInputFilter[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` on the new ObjectInputStream to [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mapply the same whitelist via `[0m[1;35mObjectInputFilter.Config.createFilter[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Modify [0m[1;35mhandleCompletedObject[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m’s JAVA_OBJDATA Branch[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Replace the naïve instantiation of `new [0m[1;35mObjectInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` with our [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`SecureObjectInputStream` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor, if running on Java [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m+, a standard ObjectInputStream [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mplus a call to `setObjectInputFilter` immediately after construction[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - On attempted deserialization of any class not in the allow-list, throw an [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`InvalidClassException` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor equivalent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m which Tika will catch and record via [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mEmbeddedDocumentUtil.recordException[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If deserialization succeeds, proceed to set `RTFMetadata.EMB_CLASS` and [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextract the object’s string bytes as before.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Preserve Fallback and Existing Behavior[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Any caught `IOException`, `ClassNotFoundException`, or `InvalidClassException`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwill be recorded in metadata by the existing exception‐handling path [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`EmbeddedDocumentUtil.recordException`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, then the handler will skip full [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextraction of that object—paralleling how OBJDATA parser errors are handled today.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This preserves existing error‐recording logic, does not break other EMB_STATE [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbranches [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOBJDATA, PICT[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and retains the “best-effort” model for embedded‐object [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextraction.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Avoid Touching Fuzz Harness or Test Code[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All changes occur within `RTFEmbObjHandler` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand the new [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`SecureObjectInputStream` helper[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. We do not modify any harness files [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`RTFParserFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m or test code, so existing fuzzer triggers and unit tests remain [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalid.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Phased Deprecation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOptional[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If supporting a granular whitelist proves complex or brittle, consider [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeprecating Java‐object deserialization entirely. In that scenario, the [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJAVA_OBJDATA case would immediately record an unsupported‐operation exception and [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextract raw bytes instead [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor skip extraction[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, to be documented in the release [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnotes.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJustification[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- By introducing an allow‐list filter at the point of deserialization, we directly [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maddress the root‐cause [0m[1;39m([0m[39munchecked readObject on untrusted data[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m without disabling [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe overall RTF parser or affecting other object types.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Overriding `resolveClass` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mJava [0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and/or using the standard `ObjectInputFilter` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAPI [0m[1;39m([0m[39mJava [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m+[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are well‐established hardening patterns for Java deserialization [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerabilities.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Catching the filter’s exceptions and delegating to [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`EmbeddedDocumentUtil.recordException` follows existing error‐handling in this code[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpath, preserving the “best‐effort” behavior without hiding other parse errors.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All other parsing logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOBJDATA, PICT, grouping in `TextExtractor`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munchanged. The fuzzer harness continues to drive parsing through the same code [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpaths, so automated tests and fuzz jobs will still exercise the protected branch [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mand now will hit the filter instead of crashing[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPotential Side Effects & Mitigations[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Legitimate RTFs embedding custom Java objects will no longer deserialize if they [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrely on disallowed classes. However, the fallback in [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`EmbeddedDocumentUtil.recordException` ensures that parsing continues and the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdocument is still indexed/extracted [0m[1;39m([0m[39malbeit without that specific object data[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The allow‐list must be carefully maintained; accidental omission of safe types [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcould break user expectations. To mitigate, start with the minimal set [0m[1;39m([0m[39mString, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprimitive wrappers[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and expand only on proven demand, logging any filtered attempts[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvia Tika’s debug‐level logging.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Document the new secure behavior clearly in the RTF parser Javadoc and the Tika  [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrelease notes, so integrators know about the tightened security model.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBy applying this targeted patch to `RTFEmbObjHandler.handleCompletedObject` and [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintroducing a small `SecureObjectInputStream` utility, we eliminate the RCE risk [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhile preserving existing functionality and test coverage. [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         == libFuzzer crashing input ==                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mReport[0m===                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         # Evaluation Report                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Summary                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         An automated security scan [1m([0mJazzer[1m)[0m flagged a remote code execution risk in the     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Apache Tika RTF parser. The failure occurred when `RTFEmbObjHandler` deserialized   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         arbitrary Java objects from RTF input via `[1;35mObjectInputStream.readObject[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m`. To      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         mitigate this, a contributor replaced the deserialization block under               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `EMB_STATE.JAVA_OBJDATA` with a call to                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[1;35mEmbeddedDocumentUtil.recordException[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m`. After applying the patch, the          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Microsoft RTF parser module fails to compile with a cascade of “illegal start of    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         type” and “class, interface, enum, or record expected” errors.                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m. Initial Issue                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - A Jazzer fuzzer invocation on the Tika RTF parser triggered                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `FuzzerSecurityIssueHigh: Remote Code Execution`.                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The stack trace pinpointed the call chain through                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[1;35mRTFEmbObjHandler.handleCompletedObject[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` and into `new                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mObjectInputStream[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m[1;35m.readObject[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m`.                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - This deserialization of attacker-controlled bytes can load arbitrary classes   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         on the classpath, enabling RCE.                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m. Key Observations in the Initial Issue                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The vulnerability resides entirely in the RTF parser’s handling of embedded    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         object data [1m([0m`JAVA_OBJDATA` state[1m)[0m.                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - No other parser modules or harness code were implicated in the crash.          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The crash is reproducible via a libFuzzer-generated input that triggers the    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[1;35mreadObject[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` path.                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m. Patch Attempt                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The contributor removed the `try [1m{[0m Object obj = new                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mObjectInputStream[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m[1;35m.readObject[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m; … [1m}[0m catch [1m([0mClassNotFoundException e[1m)[0m [1m{[0m … [1m}[0m`    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         block.                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - In its place they added:                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              ```java                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              [35m/[0m[35m/[0m Java object deserialization disabled for security                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              [1;35mEmbeddedDocumentUtil.recordException[0m[1m([0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                      new [1;35mTikaException[0m[1m([0m[32m"Java object deserialization is disabled"[0m[1m)[0m,          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         metadata[1m)[0m;                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              ```                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - This change aimed to prevent any `ObjectInputStream` invocation under          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `EMB_STATE.JAVA_OBJDATA`.                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m. Patch Result & Compilation Log                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - After patching, the module `tika-parser-microsoft-module` fails to compile.    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The reported errors [1m([0m[1;36m24[0m in total[1m)[0m include:                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • “illegal start of type”                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • “[1m<[0m[1;95midentifier[0m[39m> expected”  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • “invalid method declaration; return type required”  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • “class, interface, enum, or record expected”  [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Errors all point to line [0m[1;36m218[0m[39m of `RTFEmbObjHandler.java` and subsequent lines, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindicating misplaced or mismatched braces or incorrect code structure after the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpatch.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Areas for Further Investigation  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `RTFEmbObjHandler` class, specifically the `case EMB_STATE.JAVA_OBJDATA:` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbranch and its surrounding braces.  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Import statements and correct placement of [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mEmbeddedDocumentUtil.recordException[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Consistency of indentation and matching of `if/else if/else` blocks around [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlines [0m[1;36m211[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m220[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Any missing or extra curly braces introduced during the patch.  [0m               [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause & Symptom  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   The compilation errors stem from an extra, misplaced closing brace introduced in[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe `[0m[1;35mhandleCompletedObject[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method’s `EMB_STATE.JAVA_OBJDATA` branch. The last [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpatch replaced the unsafe `[0m[1;35mObjectInputStream.readObject[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` block but inadvertently [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39madded two successive `[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m` tokens before the next `else if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstate == EMB_STATE.NADA[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mline, unbalancing the `if`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`else if` cascade and causing “illegal start of type” [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand related syntax errors.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Critical Logic to Preserve  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The overall `if`–`else if` cascade in `[0m[1;35mhandleCompletedObject[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`:  [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       * state == OBJDATA  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       * state == PICT  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       * state == JAVA_OBJDATA  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       * state == NADA  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     must remain contiguous and correctly braced.  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The call to `[0m[1;35mreset[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` after the cascade must remain at the method’s end.  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The security mitigation—to stop any Java deserialization—must invoke [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mEmbeddedDocumentUtil.recordException[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` without throwing or re-throwing [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexceptions.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed Patch Steps  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Open `RTFEmbObjHandler.java` and locate the `[0m[1;35mhandleCompletedObject[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39maround lines [0m[1;36m211[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m225[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Identify the block:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstate == EMB_STATE.JAVA_OBJDATA[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          try [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              Object obj = new [0m[1;35mObjectInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  [0m[1;35m.readObject[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;35mmetadata.set[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m & [0m[1;35mextractObj[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mClassNotFoundException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              throw new [0m[1;35mTikaException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Not found"[0m[39m, e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstate == EMB_STATE.NADA[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Remove lines from the `try [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m` through its closing `[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39minclusive of the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`catch`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Replace them with a single call to the static helper, ensuring exactly one [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclosing brace before the next `else if`:[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstate == EMB_STATE.JAVA_OBJDATA[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Java object deserialization disabled for security[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;35mEmbeddedDocumentUtil.recordException[0m[1;39m([0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  new [0m[1;35mTikaException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Java object deserialization is disabled"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  metadata[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstate == EMB_STATE.NADA[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m swallow—no start for pict or embed?![0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   e. Confirm that the cascade now reads exactly:[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstate == EMB_STATE.OBJDATA[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[33m...[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstate == EMB_STATE.PICT[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[33m...[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstate == EMB_STATE.JAVA_OBJDATA[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;35mEmbeddedDocumentUtil.recordException[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstate == EMB_STATE.NADA[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[33m...[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;35mreset[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   f. Save and recompile to verify no syntax errors remain.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By surgically excising the deserialization logic and replacing it with a [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msingle `[0m[1;35mrecordException[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` call, we eliminate the RCE vector while preserving [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mall downstream logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe call to `[0m[1;35mextractObj[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` for other states, the final [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mreset[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, and the harness error-recording behavior[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Correcting the brace count restores valid Java syntax and re-enables [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompilation of the Microsoft RTF parser module without touching any harness or test[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode.  [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This fix follows the pattern used in the OBJDATA branch’s exception handling, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mguaranteeing consistency across states.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigation  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The JAVA_OBJDATA branch will no longer produce any embedded output beyond an [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexception record. This matches the security requirement [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdisable Java object [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeserialization[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and is explicitly documented in the code comment.  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No other states or utility methods are altered, so existing functionality for [0m [2m                [0m
